**Phase 94 ÔÇö Complete.** All 205 test modules green. Sovereign Count Sketch (CharikarÔÇôChenÔÇôFarach-Colton, 2002) ÔÇö sub-linear **frequency** estimation that, unlike Phase 76's Count-Min Sketch, gives an **unbiased** estimate. A `depth ├Ś width` integer table is paired with a *bucket* hash `h_i` and a *sign* hash `s_i Ôłł {Ôłĺ1, +1}` per row; each `(element, count)` update adds `s_i(element)┬Ěcount` to `table[i][h_i(element)]`, and a point query returns the **median** of the `depth` signed readings `table[i][h_i(x)]┬Ěs_i(x)`. The sign flip makes collision noise cancel in expectation ÔÇö the estimator is unbiased (vs Count-Min's always-positive `min`, which only over-counts). The trade-off is symmetric noise: a never-inserted element can read a small **negative** estimate when it collides with negatively-signed updates (expected and correct). The median over rows tolerates a few heavily-collided rows; updates accept **negative counts** (deletion). A side dict of every element seen powers `heavy_hitters(threshold)` (the sketch itself is not enumerable). Pure stdlib; the hash families are injectable for tests; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/count_sketch_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- Ôťů 94A: `pradyos/core/count_sketch.py` ÔÇö `CountSketchError(detail)`; `CountSketch(depth=5, width=2048, seed=0, bucket_fn=None, sign_fn=None)` with `update(element, count=1)` (count may be negative Ôćĺ deletion), `estimate(element)` (signed median; 0 for unseen in an empty table), `heavy_hitters(threshold)` Ôćĺ elements above `threshold┬Ětotal_count`, highest first, `reset(depth=None, width=None, seed=None)`, `__len__`, `depth` / `width` / `seed` / `total_count` / `unique_elements` properties, and `stats()` (depth / width / total_count / unique_elements / table_cells). Two seeded BLAKE2b hash families (bucket + sign); invalid config / non-int count raise `CountSketchError`.
- Ôťů 94B: `pradyos/web/count_sketch_web.py` ÔÇö `register_count_sketch_routes(app, count_sketch=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app sketch, depth 5 ├Ś width 2048) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/countsketch/update` (`?count=N`, default 1, may be negative; body `{element}` or `{elements: [...]}`; elements normalised to str), `GET /api/v1/countsketch/estimate` (`?element=`, required Ôćĺ 422 absent; **0 for unseen, never 422**), `GET /api/v1/countsketch/heavy_hitters` (`?threshold=`, `Query(ge=0.0, le=1.0)`), `GET /api/v1/countsketch/stats`, `POST /api/v1/countsketch/reset` (body `{depth?, width?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).
- Ôťů 94C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase94.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `count_sketch` param, and a single `register_count_sketch_routes(app, count_sketch)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- Ôťů 94D: `tests/test_count_sketch.py` (41) + `tests/test_count_sketch_web.py` (25) ÔÇö single-element **unbiasedness** (10k Ôćĺ exactly 10k, no inflation amid 5k singletons); **heavy hitters** on a Zipf stream (top-3 identified & ranked, none above 0.99, sorted desc, threshold validation); **deletion** via negative count (1000Ôłĺ300 Ôćĺ 700, delete-to-zero); **collision tolerance** (2048 elements forced into one row-0 bucket via injected hash Ôćĺ median still recovers 1); **negative estimate** for an unseen colliding element (documented trade-off); determinism (same seed Ôćĺ identical table); depth/width/seed/count validation + `CountSketchError`; stats / table_cells / reset / reconfigure; integer elements; 10-thread concurrency; all 5 endpoints incl. `?count=` deletion over HTTP + a prior-phase regression check.

**Phase 95 ÔÇö Complete.** All 207 test modules green. Sovereign Lossy Counting (MankuÔÇôMotwani, 2002) ÔÇö **deterministic** approximate frequency / heavy-hitter detection with a clean ╬Á-error guarantee and *no hashing*. The stream is divided into buckets of width `w = Ôîł1/╬ÁÔîë`, numbered `1, 2, ÔÇŽ`; a dictionary holds `{element: (freq, ╬ö)}` where `╬ö` bounds the count's under-estimate. On each arrival the element's `freq` is incremented, or it is inserted as `(count, b_current Ôłĺ 1)`; at every bucket boundary the table is swept and every entry with `freq + ╬ö ÔëĄ b_current` is deleted. This guarantees **no false negatives** (every element with true frequency Ôëą `support┬Ěn` is returned by `heavy_hitters(support)`), **no false positives above threshold** (every returned element has true frequency Ôëą `(support Ôłĺ ╬Á)┬Ěn`), and a **space bound** of `(1/╬Á)┬Ělog(╬Án)` entries. The algorithm is fully deterministic (no RNG ÔÇö `seed` is accepted for parity but unused), and **append-only**: a negative `count` raises `LossyCountError` (deletion is unsupported by design). Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/lossy_count_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- Ôťů 95A: `pradyos/core/lossy_count.py` ÔÇö `LossyCountError(detail)`; `LossyCount(epsilon=0.001, seed=None)` with `update(element, count=1)` (negative count Ôćĺ `LossyCountError("ÔÇŽdoes not support deletion")`; count=0 is a no-op), `estimate(element)` Ôćĺ tracked frequency (0 if absent), `heavy_hitters(support)` Ôćĺ elements with freq Ôëą `(support Ôłĺ ╬Á)┬Ěn`, highest first, `reset(epsilon=None, seed=None)`, `__len__`, `epsilon` / `bucket_width` / `n` / `entries` properties, and `stats()` (epsilon / n / bucket_width / entries / current_bucket). The bucket-boundary sweep loop handles batch counts crossing multiple boundaries. Invalid `epsilon` (Ôłë(0,1)) / non-int count raise `LossyCountError`.
- Ôťů 95B: `pradyos/web/lossy_count_web.py` ÔÇö `register_lossy_count_routes(app, lossy=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app counter, ╬Á=0.001) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/lossycount/update` (`?count=N`; body `{element}` or `{elements: [...]}`; **negative count Ôćĺ 422 "does not support deletion"**; elements normalised to str), `GET /api/v1/lossycount/estimate` (`?element=`, required Ôćĺ 422 absent; 0 if not retained), `GET /api/v1/lossycount/heavy_hitters` (`?support=`, `Query(gt=0, le=1.0)`), `GET /api/v1/lossycount/stats`, `POST /api/v1/lossycount/reset` (body `{epsilon?}`; 422 on bad epsilon).
- Ôťů 95C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase95.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `lossy` param, and a single `register_lossy_count_routes(app, lossy)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.

**Phase 96 ÔÇö Complete.** All 209 test modules green. Sovereign DDSketch (MassonÔÇôLee, 2019) ÔÇö a **relative-error** quantile sketch (a different guarantee from the *rank*-error sketches of Phases 91/92). Each positive value `v` is mapped to a logarithmic bucket `i = Ôîłlog_╬│(v)Ôîë` with `╬│ = (1+╬▒)/(1Ôłĺ╬▒)`, and a dict `{bucket Ôćĺ count}` tallies them; a quantile query walks the buckets in value order to the `q`-th item and returns that bucket's representative value `r_i = 2┬Ě╬│**i/(╬│+1)` (the geometric midpoint, whose worst-case relative error is exactly `(╬│Ôłĺ1)/(╬│+1) = ╬▒`). So for any quantile `q` with true value `v`, the estimate satisfies `|v╠é Ôłĺ v|/v ÔëĄ ╬▒` regardless of distribution ÔÇö ideal for long-tailed latencies where p99 accuracy matters proportionally. **Merge** adds per-bucket counts of two same-`╬▒` sketches ÔÇö *exact*, not approximate (the key differentiator over t-Digest), so distributed sketches compose losslessly. Deterministic (`seed` accepted but unused); non-positive values are rejected. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/ddsketch_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- Ôťů 96A: `pradyos/core/ddsketch.py` ÔÇö `DDSketchError(detail)`; `DDSketch(alpha=0.01, seed=None)` with `update(value, count=1)` (value > 0 or `DDSketchError("DDSketch requires positive values")`; count Ôëą 1), `quantile(q)` Ôćĺ relative-error estimate (None if empty; `DDSketchError` on qÔłë[0,1]), `merge(other)` (exact bucket-count union; same `╬▒` or `DDSketchError`), `reset(alpha=None, seed=None)`, `count()`, `__len__`, `alpha` / `gamma` / `num_buckets` properties, and `stats()` (alpha / gamma / n / num_buckets / min / max). Representative value uses the standard `2┬Ě╬│**i/(╬│+1)` (which bounds relative error by `╬▒`) ÔÇö not a naive `(1+╬▒)**i`, which mixes bases and would not bound the error. Invalid `alpha` (Ôłë(0,1)) raises `DDSketchError`.
- Ôťů 96B: `pradyos/web/ddsketch_web.py` ÔÇö `register_ddsketch_routes(app, ddsketch=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app sketch, ╬▒=0.01) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/ddsketch/update` (`?value=` `Query(gt=0)` Ôćĺ **422 on non-positive**, `?count=` `Query(ge=1)`, or body `{values: [...]}`), `GET /api/v1/ddsketch/quantile` (`?q=`, `Query(ge=0, le=1)`; **422 on empty sketch**), `POST /api/v1/ddsketch/merge` (body `{values: [...]}` Ôćĺ builds a same-`╬▒` sketch and merges it in ÔÇö the single-shared-sketch server's composability demonstration), `GET /api/v1/ddsketch/stats`, `POST /api/v1/ddsketch/reset` (body `{alpha?}`; 422 on bad alpha).
- Ôťů 96C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase96.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `ddsketch` param, and a single `register_ddsketch_routes(app, ddsketch)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- Ôťů 96D: `tests/test_ddsketch.py` (45) + `tests/test_ddsketch_web.py` (24) ÔÇö uniform & exponential & wide-range (1..1e6) streams with **every quantile level within `╬▒` relative error**; monotonicity; extremes within `╬▒`; **exact merge** (merged sketch identical to a single sketch of all values) + preserved relative error + min/max update + alpha-mismatch/non-sketch Ôćĺ `DDSketchError`; non-positive value guard (`update(0)`/`update(-1)` raise) + invalid count; determinism (seed ignored); alpha / q validation + `gamma` formula; stats / sub-linear bucket count / reset / reconfigure; floats below 1; 10-thread concurrency; all 5 endpoints incl. the merge endpoint + empty Ôćĺ 422 + a prior-phase regression check.

**Phase 97 ÔÇö Complete.** All 211 test modules green. Sovereign Exponential Histogram (DatarÔÇôGionisÔÇôIndykÔÇôMotwani, 2002) ÔÇö the first **sliding-window** primitive: how many 1-bits occurred in the last `window` ticks of a binary stream, in `O((1/╬Á)┬Ělog┬▓(window))` space (it never stores the raw stream). The window is summarised by buckets `(timestamp, size=2ßÁĆ)` ordered oldestÔćĺnewest; each update appends a size-1 bucket at the current tick, then ÔÇö while more than `k = Ôîł1/╬ÁÔîë` buckets share a size ÔÇö merges the two **oldest** of that size into one of double the size (taking the newer timestamp); buckets older than `window` ticks expire. `count()` returns `╬ú size Ôłĺ ┬Ż┬Ě(oldest bucket size)` (the DGIM end-correction, since the oldest bucket may straddle the boundary), estimating the windowed count with **relative error ÔëĄ ╬Á/2** (empirically validated). Deterministic (`seed` accepted but unused); a binary-stream model (`value` = number of 1-bits at a tick; no fractional/weighted updates). Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/exponential_histogram_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- Ôťů 97A: `pradyos/core/exponential_histogram.py` ÔÇö `ExponentialHistogramError(detail)`; `ExponentialHistogram(window, epsilon=0.5, seed=None)` with `update(value=1, timestamp=None)` (value Ôëą 1 1-bits; timestamp defaults to the next internal tick, must be non-decreasing else `ExponentialHistogramError`), `count()` Ôćĺ DGIM windowed estimate, `oldest()` Ôćĺ oldest surviving bucket timestamp (None if empty), `reset(window=None, epsilon=None, seed=None)`, `__len__`, `window` / `epsilon` / `k` / `now` / `num_buckets` properties, and `stats()` (window / epsilon / k / num_buckets / count / oldest / now). Invalid `window` (ÔëĄ0) / `epsilon` (Ôłë(0,1]) raise `ExponentialHistogramError`.
- Ôťů 97B: `pradyos/web/exponential_histogram_web.py` ÔÇö `register_exponential_histogram_routes(app, histogram=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app histogram, window=1000) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/window/update` (`?value=` `Query(ge=1)`, `?timestamp=` `Query(ge=0)`; **422 on non-monotone timestamp**), `GET /api/v1/window/count`, `GET /api/v1/window/oldest`, `GET /api/v1/window/stats`, `POST /api/v1/window/reset` (`?window=` `Query(gt=0)`, `?epsilon=` `Query(gt=0, le=1)`; 422 on bad params).
- Ôťů 97C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase97.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `exp_histogram` param, and a single `register_exponential_histogram_routes(app, exp_histogram)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- Ôťů 97D: `tests/test_exponential_histogram.py` (42) + `tests/test_exponential_histogram_web.py` (20) ÔÇö dense count within `╬Á/2` (incl. the directive's window=500/╬Á=0.5 scenario, tighter ╬Á, and sub-window n); **sliding expiry** (200 then advance 600 then 100 Ôćĺ ~100); old-buckets-expire + expiry invariant + oldest-advances; **merge invariant** (ÔëĄ `k+1` buckets per size after every update) + power-of-two sizes + poly-log space; explicit timestamps + multi-bit `value`; determinism (seed ignored); window/epsilon/value/non-monotone-timestamp validation + `ExponentialHistogramError`; stats / reset / reconfigure; the single-bit DGIM end-correction (`count`=0.5); 10-thread concurrency; all 5 endpoints incl. sliding expiry over HTTP + a prior-phase regression check.

**Phase 98 ÔÇö Complete.** All 213 test modules green. Sovereign Weighted Reservoir Sampling (EfraimidisÔÇôSpirakis "A-Res", 2006) ÔÇö a random sample of `k` items from a stream of `(item, weight)` pairs in one pass and `O(k)` space, where an item is retained with probability **proportional to its weight** (unlike Phase 85's *uniform* Algorithm R). Each arrival gets a priority key `u**(1/weight)` (`u Ôł╝ Uniform(0,1)`); a **min-heap** keeps the `k` items with the largest keys (push while under capacity, else replace the smallest if beaten). Heavier weights drive `1/weight` toward 0 and thus the key toward 1, so heavy items win more ÔÇö verified empirically at a ~96:1 selection ratio for weight 100 vs 1. This is the first **randomized** primitive in a while: a seeded `random.Random` makes it reproducible/injectable. `reset()` clears the reservoir but deliberately does *not* re-seed the RNG (the generator state continues ÔÇö correct for a long-lived sampler). A counter tiebreaker `(key, counter, item)` means the heap never compares items, so any item type is safe. Weights must be positive; `k Ôëą 1`. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/weighted_reservoir_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- Ôťů 98A: `pradyos/core/weighted_reservoir.py` ÔÇö `WeightedReservoirError(detail)`; `WeightedReservoir(k, seed=0)` with `update(item, weight=1.0)` (weight > 0 or `WeightedReservoirError("weight must be positive")`), `sample()` Ôćĺ reservoir contents (`[]` if empty, order not guaranteed), `reset()` (clears; RNG continues), `__len__`, `k` / `seed` / `n` / `size` properties, and `stats()` (k / n / size / seed). `k < 1` raises `WeightedReservoirError("k must be at least 1")`. No `merge` ÔÇö A-Res reservoirs are not composable.
- Ôťů 98B: `pradyos/web/weighted_reservoir_web.py` ÔÇö `register_weighted_reservoir_routes(app, reservoir=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app sampler, k=100) mounts 4 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/sample/update` (`?item=` required str, `?weight=` `Query(gt=0)` Ôćĺ **422 on non-positive**), `GET /api/v1/sample/sample` (`{items, n, k}`), `GET /api/v1/sample/stats`, `POST /api/v1/sample/reset`.
- Ôťů 98C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase98.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `weighted_reservoir` param, and a single `register_weighted_reservoir_routes(app, weighted_reservoir)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- Ôťů 98D: `tests/test_weighted_reservoir.py` (35) + `tests/test_weighted_reservoir_web.py` (18) ÔÇö capacity fills to `k` (10k items Ôćĺ 50) / under-capacity keeps all / exactly-k; **weight-proportional bias** (weight 100 selected >10├Ś weight 1; top-10 by frequency all from the top-20 by weight) + uniform-weights-unbiased; determinism (same seed Ôćĺ identical reservoir) + different-seed-differs; **reset does not re-seed the RNG** (replay diverges from a fresh same-seed reservoir); weight guard (0 / negative / non-number raise) + `k`/`seed` validation + `WeightedReservoirError`; arbitrary non-comparable item types (counter tiebreaker); stats / reset / refill; 10-thread concurrency; all 4 endpoints incl. injected capacity + a high-weight-retained check + a prior-phase regression check.

**Phase 99 ÔÇö Complete.** All 215 test modules green. Sovereign Misra-Gries (MisraÔÇôGries, 1982) ÔÇö the original **deterministic counter-based heavy-hitter** algorithm. At most `k` monitored `(item Ôćĺ count)` counters are kept: on a hit increment; on a new item with a free slot start a counter; otherwise **decrement every counter** by the item's count and drop those that reach zero (the arriving item is absorbed by that decrement, not stored). This is the distinctive Misra-Gries step ÔÇö compared with Space-Saving's *evict-minimum* (P87) and Lossy Counting's *window-sweep* (P95). Guarantees: any element with true frequency `> n/(k+1)` is retained; every reported count under-estimates the true frequency by at most `n/(k+1)`; space is exactly `k` counters. So `heavy_hitters(support)` (counts `Ôëą (support Ôłĺ 1/(k+1))┬Ěn`) has no false negatives among elements with true frequency `Ôëą support┬Ěn` **provided `support > 1/(k+1)`** (a larger `k` covers smaller support). Deterministic (no RNG ÔÇö `seed` accepted but unused); append-only (non-positive `count` raises `MisraGriesError`). Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/misra_gries_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- Ôťů 99A: `pradyos/core/misra_gries.py` ÔÇö `MisraGriesError(detail)`; `MisraGries(k, seed=None)` with `update(element, count=1)` (count Ôëą 1; non-positive Ôćĺ `MisraGriesError("Misra-Gries does not support deletion")`), `estimate(element)` Ôćĺ stored under-count (0 if absent), `heavy_hitters(support)` Ôćĺ elements with count `Ôëą (support Ôłĺ 1/(k+1))┬Ěn`, highest first, `reset(k=None)`, `__len__`, `k` / `n` / `counters` properties, and `stats()` (k / n / counters / `threshold = n/(k+1)`). `k < 1` raises `MisraGriesError("k must be at least 1")`.
- Ôťů 99B: `pradyos/web/misra_gries_web.py` ÔÇö `register_misra_gries_routes(app, misra=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app counter, k=100) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/misragries/update` (`?count=` `Query(ge=1)` Ôćĺ **422 on non-positive (the no-deletion guard)**; body `{element}` or `{elements: [...]}`), `GET /api/v1/misragries/estimate` (`?element=`, required Ôćĺ 422 absent), `GET /api/v1/misragries/heavy_hitters` (`?support=`, `Query(gt=0, le=1)`), `GET /api/v1/misragries/stats`, `POST /api/v1/misragries/reset` (body `{k?}`; 422 on bad k).
- Ôťů 99C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase99.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `misra_gries` param, and a single `register_misra_gries_routes(app, misra_gries)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- Ôťů 99D: `tests/test_misra_gries.py` (40) + `tests/test_misra_gries_web.py` (25) ÔÇö Zipf no-false-negatives at `support=0.05` with `k=20` (so `support > 1/(k+1)`) + correct ranking; the **rigorous retention guarantee** (every element with freq `> n/(k+1)` retained, tested at `k=10`); under-count bounded by `n/(k+1)`; estimate never over-counts; the **decrement-all** step (a,b,c at k=2 Ôćĺ empty table; batch `a├Ś5, b├Ś3, c-miss├Ś2 Ôćĺ a=3, b=1`); counter cap ÔëĄ k; monitored-increment / free-slot-insert; no-deletion guard (count 0 / negative / non-int raise); determinism (seed ignored); k validation + `MisraGriesError`; support validation; stats / `threshold` / reset / reconfigure; integer elements; 10-thread concurrency; all 5 endpoints incl. the Zipf no-false-negative check over HTTP + a prior-phase regression check.

**Phase 100 ÔÇö Complete. ­čÄ» Centennial.** All 217 test modules green. Sovereign XOR Filter (GrafÔÇôLemire, 2020) ÔÇö a **static, space-optimal** approximate-membership filter that beats Bloom (P72) and Cuckoo (P86) on lookup speed (exactly **three memory probes, no search**) and is built **once** from a complete key set (then immutable ÔÇö the design difference from the incremental Bloom and Cuckoo). Each key maps to three buckets `h0, h1, h2` (one per segment); a **peeling** construction repeatedly removes a key that owns a bucket no other unassigned key touches, then assigns fingerprints in reverse peel order so `F[b] = fingerprint(k) ÔŐĽ F[other1] ÔŐĽ F[other2]` ÔÇö making `fingerprint(k) == F[h0] ÔŐĽ F[h1] ÔŐĽ F[h2]` hold for every built key (zero false negatives). A non-member matches with probability `Ôëł 2**-bits_per_entry` (Ôëł 0.4 % at 8 bits, 0 observed at 16 bits over 10 000 queries). Fingerprints are the low `bits_per_entry` bits of a seeded BLAKE2b digest. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/xor_filter_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- Ôťů 100A: `pradyos/core/xor_filter.py` ÔÇö `XorFilterError(detail)`; `XorFilter(bits_per_entry=8, seed=0)` with `build(keys)` (static; dedups; replaces any prior filter; `XorFilterError("peeling failed ÔÇö retry with different seed")` on a rare stall), `contains(key)` (`XorFilterError("filter not built ÔÇö call build() first")` before build), `reset(bits_per_entry=None, seed=None)`, `__contains__`, `__len__`, `bits_per_entry` / `seed` / `built` / `array_size` properties, and `stats()` (bits_per_entry / built / n / array_size / segment_size / `false_positive_rate = 2**-bits`). Invalid `bits_per_entry` (Ôłë[1,64]) / `seed` raise `XorFilterError`.
- Ôťů 100B: `pradyos/web/xor_filter_web.py` ÔÇö `register_xor_filter_routes(app, xor=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app filter, 8-bit, unbuilt) mounts 4 (all-static) routes ÔÇö **no insert (the filter is static)**: `POST /api/v1/xorfilter/build` (body `{keys: [...]}`; 422 on missing / non-list / peeling failure), `GET /api/v1/xorfilter/contains` (`?key=`; **422 before build**), `GET /api/v1/xorfilter/stats`, `POST /api/v1/xorfilter/reset` (body `{bits_per_entry?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).
- Ôťů 100C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase100.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `xor_filter` param, and a single `register_xor_filter_routes(app, xor_filter)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- Ôťů 100D: `tests/test_xor_filter.py` (39) + `tests/test_xor_filter_web.py` (20) ÔÇö membership (10 000 keys all contained, zero false negatives); 8-bit FPR `< 1/128` & 16-bit FPR `0`/10 000 & wider-fingerprint-fewer-FPs; **static constraint** (contains before build / after reset raises); **rebuild replaces** (set A Ôćĺ set B; A survives only at FP level); `build` dedups; determinism (same seed Ôćĺ identical array) + different-seed-differs; **peeling robustness** (0 failures across 20 varied key sets at one seed); bits / seed validation + `XorFilterError`; stats / FPR formula / reset / reconfigure; integer & mixed key types; 10-thread concurrent membership; all 4 endpoints incl. build Ôćĺ contains over HTTP + a prior-phase regression check.
- Ôťů 100E: `scripts/prove.py` ÔÇö 217 test modules registered (Phase 100 appends `test_xor_filter.py` + `test_xor_filter_web.py`).
- Ôťů 100F: README Phase Map updated; Phase 101 planned.

**Phase 101 ÔÇö Complete.** All 219 test modules green. Sovereign Ribbon Filter (DillingerÔÇôWalzer, 2021) ÔÇö the **retrieval-based** static membership filter that succeeds the XOR filter (P100) with better space efficiency: it frames membership as a **sparse linear system over GF(2)** and solves it down a narrow diagonal *ribbon* band rather than by peeling. Each key maps to a start column `s(k) Ôłł [0, m-w]`, a `w`-bit coefficient row `c(k)` anchored at `s` (bit 0 forced to 1), and a `bits_per_entry`-bit fingerprint `f(k)`; its equation is `ÔŐĽ_{j: c(k)[j]=1} Z[s(k)+j] = f(k)` over a slot table `Z`. Rows are reduced into an incremental row-echelon form keyed by pivot column (each insert shifts to its leftmost set bit and, if that pivot is occupied, XORs against the resident row ÔÇö the band never widens past `w`, so each insert is `O(w)`), then a back-substitution from the high column down fills `Z`. A query recomputes `s, c` and XORs the selected slots, so `ÔŐĽ Z[s+j] == f(k)` holds for every built key (**zero false negatives**); a non-member matches only by fingerprint collision (`Ôëł 2**-bits`, Ôëł 0.4 % at 8 bits, 0 observed at 16 bits over 10 000 queries). With ribbon width `w = 64` and target load `0.85`, the table is `m = Ôîłn / 0.85Ôîë + w` slots ÔÇö an overhead of **Ôëł 1.18├Ś at scale, below the XOR filter's 1.23├Ś theoretical bound and far below its 3.69├Ś peeling construction**; wider `w` pushes the load toward the `n ┬Ě bits` limit. If a row reduces to zero coefficients with a non-zero residual the system is singular ÔÇö `RibbonFilterError` asks for a different seed (astronomically rare at load 0.85). Fingerprint / start / coefficient are slices of a seeded BLAKE2b digest. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock` (the heavy solve runs lock-free on a snapshot, published with one locked assignment). Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/ribbon_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- Ôťů 101A: `pradyos/core/ribbon.py` ÔÇö `RibbonFilterError(detail)`; `RibbonFilter(bits_per_entry=8, seed=0)` with `build(keys)` (static; dedups; replaces any prior filter; `RibbonFilterError("construction failed ÔÇö linearly dependent rows (retry with different seed)")` on a singular system; empty build is valid and contains nothing), `contains(key)` (`RibbonFilterError("filter not built ÔÇö call build() first")` before build), `reset(bits_per_entry=None, seed=None)`, `__contains__`, `__len__`, `bits_per_entry` / `seed` / `built` / `slots` / `ribbon_width` properties, and `stats()` (bits_per_entry / built / n / slots / ribbon_width / load_factor / `false_positive_rate = 2**-bits`). Invalid `bits_per_entry` (Ôłë[1,64]) / `seed` raise `RibbonFilterError`.
- Ôťů 101B: `pradyos/web/ribbon_web.py` ÔÇö `register_ribbon_routes(app, ribbon=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app filter, 8-bit, unbuilt) mounts 4 (all-static) routes ÔÇö **no insert (the filter is static)**: `POST /api/v1/ribbon/build` (body `{keys: [...]}`; 422 on missing / non-list / singular-system), `GET /api/v1/ribbon/contains` (`?key=`; **422 before build**), `GET /api/v1/ribbon/stats`, `POST /api/v1/ribbon/reset` (body `{bits_per_entry?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).

**Phase 102 ÔÇö Complete.** All 221 test modules green. Sovereign HeavyKeeper (Gong et al., 2018) ÔÇö a probabilistic **heavy-hitter / top-K frequency** sketch (pivot: the originally-eyed Count-Min Sketch was already shipped at P76 ÔÇö `class CountMinSketch` ÔÇö so Phase 102 stays in the frequency family but ships a genuinely-new algorithm). It keeps a `depth ├Ś width` grid of `(fingerprint, count)` cells (`count == 0` marks empty); for each occurrence of an item `x` (fingerprint `f = fp(x)`), every row hashes `x` to a cell and applies **exponential-decay-on-collision**: an empty cell is claimed `(f, 1)`, a matching fingerprint does `count += 1`, and a *mismatching* cell decays the resident only with probability `decay ** -count` ÔÇö evicting and re-claiming it when the count hits 0. Because a genuine heavy hitter's count is large, `decay ** -count` is minuscule, so it is almost never decayed while cold items evaporate fast. The frequency estimate is the **max** matching counter across rows (not the *min*, as in Count-Min P76 ÔÇö decay makes over-counting the failure mode to guard), and a bounded **indexed min-heap of size k** (`O(log k)` updates) tracks the live top-K, replacing its minimum only when exceeded. This decay rule is the distinctive mechanism ÔÇö versus Count-Min's *min counters* (P76), Count Sketch's *signed estimate* (P94), Space-Saving's *evict-minimum* (P87), Misra-Gries' *decrement-all* (P99) and Lossy Counting's *window-sweep* (P95). Hashing is seeded BLAKE2b; the decay draws from a seeded `random.Random` so `seed` + stream is fully deterministic. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/heavykeeper_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- Ôťů 102A: `pradyos/core/heavykeeper.py` ÔÇö `HeavyKeeperError(detail)`; `HeavyKeeper(k=10, width=1024, depth=4, decay=1.08, seed=0)` with `add(item, count=1)` (returns the updated estimate; reconciles the top-K heap), `query(item)` (max matching counter, 0 if absent), `top_k(n=None)` (`(item, estimate)` sorted by estimate desc; defaults to `k`), `reset(k=None, width=None, depth=None, decay=None, seed=None)` (clears buckets + heap; optional reconfigure), `__len__` (tracked count), `k`/`width`/`depth`/`decay`/`seed` properties, and `stats()` (k / width / depth / decay / seed / tracked / total). Invalid `k`/`width`/`depth` (Ôłë ÔäĄÔü║), `decay` (ÔëĄ 1) or `seed` / non-positive `count` raise `HeavyKeeperError`.
- Ôťů 102B: `pradyos/web/heavykeeper_web.py` ÔÇö `register_heavykeeper_routes(app, heavykeeper=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app sketch) mounts 4 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/heavykeeper/add` (body `{item, count?}`; 422 on missing item / bad count), `GET /api/v1/heavykeeper/topk` (`?n=` with `Query(ge=1)` Ôćĺ auto-422; defaults to `k`), `GET /api/v1/heavykeeper/stats`, `POST /api/v1/heavykeeper/reset` (body `{k?, width?, depth?, decay?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).
- Ôťů 102C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase102.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `heavykeeper` param, and a single `register_heavykeeper_routes(app, heavykeeper)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- Ôťů 102D: `tests/test_heavykeeper.py` (41) + `tests/test_heavykeeper_web.py` (20) ÔÇö **heavy-hitter detection** (1 @ 1000 + 9 @ 100 in a 10 000 stream Ôćĺ all 10 in `top_k(10)`); **frequency accuracy** (top item within 20 % of 1000); **eviction** (freq < 5 noise never in top-K); **decay sensitivity** (decay 1.02 forgets faster Ôćĺ less surviving bucket mass & lower hot-item counts than 1.5); **estimate = max not min**; determinism (same seed + stream Ôćĺ identical top-K, survives reset); top-K bounded by `k` / sorted desc / `n` param / keeps-largest; config + `count` validation + `HeavyKeeperError.detail`; stats / reset / reconfigure; integer & mixed items; 8-thread concurrent adds (heap ÔëĄ k, index map consistent, dominant hitter retained); all 4 endpoints over HTTP + a prior-phase regression check.
- Ôťů 102E: `scripts/prove.py` ÔÇö 221 test modules registered (Phase 102 appends `test_heavykeeper.py` + `test_heavykeeper_web.py`).

**Phase 103 ÔÇö Complete.** All 223 test modules green. Sovereign Spectral Bloom Filter (Cohen & Matias, 2003) ÔÇö a **frequency-aware** Bloom filter that replaces the standard filter's single presence *bit* (P12) with an array of integer **counters**, estimating an item's multiplicity as the **minimum** counter across its `k` hash positions. That minimum is the natural estimator and the exact counterpoint to HeavyKeeper's *max* (P102): collisions can only push a counter higher, so the smallest of an item's counters is the tightest estimate and over-counting (never under-counting) is the only failure mode ÔÇö zero false negatives, like any Bloom. Because the cells are counters, it also supports **deletion**: `remove` decrements an item's counters (guarded so a non-member, whose minimum is already 0, is never touched and counters never go negative) ÔÇö the practical edge over a plain Bloom. Sizing uses the standard Bloom formulae from `capacity` and `error_rate`: `m = Ôîł-capacity┬Ěln(error_rate)/ln(2)┬▓Ôîë` counter slots and `k = round((m/capacity)┬Ěln2)` hashes, so membership FPR (`min > 0`) equals a standard Bloom's. The `k` positions come from one seeded BLAKE2b digest split into two 64-bit halves combined by KirschÔÇôMitzenmacher double hashing (`h1 + i┬Ěh2 mod m`), deterministic per `seed`. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/spectralbloom_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- Ôťů 103A: `pradyos/core/spectral_bloom.py` ÔÇö `SpectralBloomError(detail)`; `SpectralBloom(capacity=10000, error_rate=0.01, seed=0)` with `add(element, count=1)` (returns the updated multiplicity estimate), `query(element)` (min counter; 0 if absent), `remove(element, count=1)` (removes up to `count` occurrences only if present; returns the number removed; guards Ôëą 0), `reset(capacity=None, error_rate=None, seed=None)` (clears; re-derives `m`/`k`), `__contains__` (min > 0), `__len__` (net occurrences), `capacity`/`error_rate`/`seed`/`num_bits`/`num_hashes` properties, and `stats()` (capacity / error_rate / num_bits / num_hashes / num_added / estimated_fill_ratio). Invalid `capacity` (Ôłë ÔäĄÔü║), `error_rate` (Ôłë (0,1)) or `seed`, and non-positive `count`, raise `SpectralBloomError`.
- Ôťů 103B: `pradyos/web/spectralbloom_web.py` ÔÇö `register_spectralbloom_routes(app, spectral=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app filter) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/spectralbloom/add` (body `{item, count?}`), `GET /api/v1/spectralbloom/query` (`?item=` Ôćĺ auto-422 if absent), `DELETE /api/v1/spectralbloom/remove` (body `{item, count?}` ÔÇö deletion), `GET /api/v1/spectralbloom/stats`, `POST /api/v1/spectralbloom/reset` (body `{capacity?, error_rate?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).
- Ôťů 103C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase103.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `spectral_bloom` param, and a single `register_spectralbloom_routes(app, spectral_bloom)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- Ôťů 103D: `tests/test_spectral_bloom.py` (43) + `tests/test_spectralbloom_web.py` (21) ÔÇö **zero false negatives** (1 000 members all query Ôëą 1); **FPR ÔëĄ 2 ├Ś error_rate** (and near-0 under-loaded); **multiplicity exact at low load** (add ├Ś5 Ôćĺ query 5; batch `add(x, 7)`); **estimate = min not max**; **deletion** (add 3 Ôćĺ remove Ôćĺ 2 Ôćĺ remove to 0/not-member; remove non-member is a no-op that never corrupts shared counters; over-remove clamped); standard Bloom sizing (`m`/`k` formulae; smaller error_rate grows `m`); determinism (same seed Ôćĺ identical positions, survives reset); config + `count` validation + `SpectralBloomError.detail`; stats / num_added / fill_ratio / reset / reconfigure; membership operator; integer & mixed items; 8-thread concurrent adds (no lost increments); all 5 endpoints incl. `DELETE`-with-body over HTTP + a prior-phase regression check.

**Phase 104 ÔÇö Complete.** All 225 test modules green. Sovereign Augmented Sketch / ASketch (Roy, Khan & Pomerantz, 2016) ÔÇö a **two-stage frequency** estimator that bolts a small *exact* filter of the current heavy hitters onto a sketch base (pivot: the directive's eyed Cuckoo Filter is already shipped at P86 ÔÇö `class CuckooFilter`, `/api/v1/cuckoo` ÔÇö so Phase 104 ships a genuinely-new structure). **Stage 1** is a **Count Sketch** base (CharikarÔÇôChenÔÇôFarach-Colton 2002), *not* Count-Min (P76): each of `depth` rows maps an item to a bucket and an independent **sign** `s Ôłł {+1,-1}`, `add` does `counter[d][j] += s┬Ědelta`, and the estimate is the **median** of `s┬Ěcounter[d][j]` across rows ÔÇö a *signed median*, so colliding items contribute `┬▒` and cancel in expectation (an *unbiased* estimate), where Count-Min's min only ever over-counts. **Stage 2** is an exact-count dict of ÔëĄ `k` items: on `add`, a tracked item's count is bumped exactly, otherwise the sketch is updated and the item is **promoted** (evicting the dict minimum when full) once its sketch estimate exceeds the smallest tracked count; `query` returns the exact dict count when tracked, else the sketch median, and `top_k` reads exact counts straight off the dict. Hashing is seeded BLAKE2b (one digest per row Ôćĺ bucket + sign bit). Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/augmentedsketch_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- Ôťů 104A: `pradyos/core/augmented_sketch.py` ÔÇö `AugmentedSketchError(detail)`; `AugmentedSketch(width=1024, depth=4, k=10, seed=0)` with `add(item, delta=1)` (returns updated estimate; promotes into the dict), `query(item)` (exact if tracked, else signed-median sketch estimate), `sketch_estimate(item)` (the Count Sketch base estimate alone), `top_k(n=None)` (`(item, exact_count)` desc; defaults to `k`), `reset(width=None, depth=None, k=None, seed=None)`, `__len__` (tracked count), `width`/`depth`/`k`/`seed` properties, and `stats()` (width / depth / k / seed / tracked / total). Invalid `width`/`depth`/`k` (Ôłë ÔäĄÔü║) or `seed`, and non-positive `delta`, raise `AugmentedSketchError`.
- Ôťů 104B: `pradyos/web/augmentedsketch_web.py` ÔÇö `register_augmentedsketch_routes(app, augmented=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app sketch) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/augmentedsketch/add` (body `{item, delta?}`; 422 on missing item / bad delta), `GET /api/v1/augmentedsketch/query` (`?item=` Ôćĺ auto-422 if absent), `GET /api/v1/augmentedsketch/topk` (`?n=` with `Query(ge=1)`; defaults to `k`), `GET /api/v1/augmentedsketch/stats`, `POST /api/v1/augmentedsketch/reset` (body `{width?, depth?, k?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).
- Ôťů 104C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase104.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `augmented_sketch` param, and a single `register_augmentedsketch_routes(app, augmented_sketch)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- Ôťů 104D: `tests/test_augmented_sketch.py` (39) + `tests/test_augmentedsketch_web.py` (22) ÔÇö **heavy-hitter detection** (1 @ 1000 + 4 @ 100 in a 10 000 stream Ôćĺ all in `top_k`, counts within 50 of true since promoted); **sketch quality** (mid-frequency signed-median within ~30 %); **sign cancellation** (Count Sketch base estimate of an item stays Ôëł its true count under heavy colliding noise ÔÇö not inflated as Count-Min's min would be); **promotion** (a riser transitions from sketch estimate to exact dict count; a light item is not promoted past a full dict); top-K bounded by `k` / sorted desc / `n` param / keeps-largest; determinism (same seed + stream Ôćĺ identical top-K and sketch array; survives reset); config + `delta` validation + `AugmentedSketchError.detail`; stats / reset / reconfigure; integer & mixed items; 8-thread concurrent adds (dict ÔëĄ k, dominant hitter retained); all 5 endpoints over HTTP + a prior-phase regression check.

**Phase 105 ÔÇö Complete.** All 227 test modules green. Sovereign Q-Digest (Shrivastava, Buragohain, Agrawal & Suri, 2004) ÔÇö a **mergeable quantile sketch** for streaming percentile estimation (p50/p95/p99). It lays a *complete binary tree* over the value universe `[0, value_range)` (rounded up to a power-of-two capacity so the tree is complete), each node spanning `[lower, upper)`; only nodes with a positive count are stored (a `dict` keyed by heap-numbered node id), so the empty regions of a sparse universe cost nothing. `add` increments the value's leaf, then **compresses**: with `n` total elements and factor `k` the threshold is `ÔîŐn/kÔîő`, and the tree is swept bottom-up merging any node/sibling/parent triple whose summed count falls below it up into the parent ÔÇö enforcing the digest property and bounding the structure to `O(k┬Ělog ¤â)` nodes (`¤â = value_range`). `quantile(q)` walks stored nodes by increasing upper boundary, accumulating counts until the running sum reaches `q┬Ěn`, and reports that node's max value; `rank(v)` sums counts of nodes lying entirely at/below `v`; `merge` adds node counts of two same-universe digests and recompresses (ideal for distributed aggregation). Fully deterministic (no randomness; the `seed` is carried for API parity and reported in stats). *(Pivot note: the directive's eyed **t-Digest is already shipped at Phase 79** ÔÇö `class TDigest`, `/api/v1/tdigest` ÔÇö and **DDSketch at Phase 96** ÔÇö `/api/v1/ddsketch`; both quantile sketches collide, so Phase 105 ships a genuinely-new one, distinct from those plus Greenwald-Khanna (P91) and KLL (P92) ÔÇö a tree/domain-decomposition approach.)* Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/qdigest_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- Ôťů 105A: `pradyos/core/q_digest.py` ÔÇö `QDigestError(detail)`; `QDigest(compression_factor=100, value_range=65536, seed=0)` with `add(value, count=1)` (range-checked; recompresses), `quantile(q)` (`q` strictly in (0,1); `QDigestError` on empty / bad `q`), `rank(value)`, `merge(other)` (same-universe node-wise add + recompress; returns self; does not mutate `other`), `reset(compression_factor=None, value_range=None, seed=None)`, `__len__` (total count), `compression_factor`/`value_range`/`seed`/`num_nodes`/`total_count` properties, and `stats()` (compression_factor / value_range / total_count / num_nodes / theoretical_max_nodes = `k┬Ělog ¤â`). Invalid config, out-of-range / non-int value, or non-positive count raise `QDigestError`.
- Ôťů 105B: `pradyos/web/qdigest_web.py` ÔÇö `register_qdigest_routes(app, qdigest=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app digest) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/qdigest/add` (body `{value, count?}`; 422 on missing value / out-of-range / bad count), `GET /api/v1/qdigest/quantile` (`?q=` with `Query(gt=0.0, lt=1.0)`; **422 on empty digest**), `POST /api/v1/qdigest/merge` (body `{values: [...]}` Ôćĺ builds a temp digest and merges it in), `GET /api/v1/qdigest/stats`, `POST /api/v1/qdigest/reset` (body `{compression_factor?, value_range?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).
- Ôťů 105C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase105.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `qdigest` param, and a single `register_qdigest_routes(app, qdigest)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- Ôťů 105D: `tests/test_q_digest.py` (64) + `tests/test_qdigest_web.py` (24) ÔÇö **uniform p50** (10 000 values over [0,1000) Ôćĺ p50 Ôłł [475,525]); **tail p99** within 5 % of 990; **merge correctness** (two 5 000-value halves Ôćĺ merged p50 within 5 % of true); **compression bound** (`num_nodes ÔëĄ 4┬Ěk┬ĚlogÔéé(value_range)`); **strict monotonicity** of `quantile(0.25..0.99)`; **determinism** (same seed + values + order Ôćĺ identical tree and quantiles); low-count full-resolution (n < k Ôćĺ no merging); rank monotonicity; skewed-distribution accuracy; config / value / count / `q` validation + `QDigestError.detail`; stats / reset / reconfigure; 8-thread concurrent adds; all 5 endpoints over HTTP + a prior-phase regression check.

**Phase 106 ÔÇö Complete.** All 229 test modules green. Sovereign Moment Sketch (Gan, Ding, Tai, Sheng, Bailis & Madden, 2018) ÔÇö a **mergeable quantile sketch** that summarises a stream by its first `k` *power-sum moments* `C[i] = ╬ú xÔü▒` (`i = 0..k-1`) together with the observed `min` / `max`. Quantiles are reconstructed at query time by fitting a **maximum-entropy (MaxEnt)** distribution to the moments: among all densities on `[min, max]` whose moments match the observed ones, the maximum-entropy choice is `p(x) ÔłŁ exp(╬úÔ▒╝ ╬╗Ô▒╝┬Ěx╩▓)`, with the values rescaled to the Chebyshev domain `[-1, 1]` for conditioning and the Lagrange multipliers `╬╗` solved by minimising the convex dual potential `log Ôłź exp(╬úÔ▒╝ ╬╗Ô▒╝ x╩▓) dx Ôłĺ ╬úÔ▒╝ ╬╗Ô▒╝ ╬╝Ô▒╝` (gradient = fitted Ôłĺ empirical moment) via `scipy.optimize.minimize` (L-BFGS-B). `quantile(q)` integrates the fitted density to a CDF and inverts it to find `v` with `CDF(v) = q`. Power sums are **trivially mergeable** ÔÇö element-wise addition plus `min`/`max` of bounds ÔÇö so distributed partitions combine in constant time. Fully deterministic (no randomness; `seed` carried for API parity). *(Collision note: the directive's originally-eyed **KLL Sketch is already shipped at Phase 92** ÔÇö `class KLLSketch`, `pradyos/core/kll_sketch.py`, `/api/v1/kll` ÔÇö so `kll_sketch` / `KLLSketch` read non-zero and were not reused; Phase 106 ships Moment Sketch instead.)* Depends on `numpy` / `scipy` (declared in `pyproject.toml`); thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/moment_sketch_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- Ôťů 106A: `pradyos/core/moment_sketch.py` ÔÇö `MomentSketchError(detail)`; `MomentSketch(k=15, seed=0)` with `add(x)` (updates each power sum + min/max), `add_many(values)`, `quantile(q)` (`q` strictly in (0,1); MaxEnt fit; `MomentSketchError` on empty / bad `q`), `merge(other)` (same-`k` element-wise add + min/max; returns self; does not mutate `other`), `merge_state(dict)` / `from_state(dict)` (serialized-state round-trip), `reset(k=None, seed=None)`, `__len__` (= C[0]), `k`/`seed`/`total_count` properties, and `stats()` (k / seed / total_count / min_val / max_val / moments). Invalid `k`/`seed`, non-numeric value, or mismatched-`k` merge raise `MomentSketchError`.
- Ôťů 106B: `pradyos/web/moment_sketch_web.py` ÔÇö `register_momentsketch_routes(app, sketch=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app sketch) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/momentsketch/add` (body `{value}`; 422 on missing / non-numeric value), `GET /api/v1/momentsketch/quantile` (`?q=` with `Query(gt=0.0, lt=1.0)`; **422 on empty sketch**), `POST /api/v1/momentsketch/merge` (body = a serialized `stats()` state with a `moments` list Ôćĺ reconstructs and merges), `GET /api/v1/momentsketch/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/momentsketch/reset` (body `{k?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).
- Ôťů 106C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase106.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `moment_sketch` param, and a single `register_momentsketch_routes(app, moment_sketch)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- Ôťů 106D: `tests/test_moment_sketch.py` (61) + `tests/test_moment_sketch_web.py` (23) ÔÇö **uniform p50** (10 000 values over [0,1000) Ôćĺ p50 Ôłł [475,525]); **tail p99** within 5 % of 990; **merge correctness** (two 5 000-value complementary halves Ôćĺ merged p50 within 5 % of true); **strict monotonicity** of `quantile(0.25..0.99)`; **determinism** (same values + order Ôćĺ identical power sums and quantiles); **moment consistency** (C[0] = exact count; C[1]/C[0] = sample mean within 1 %; power sums match `╬úxÔü▒` by definition); skewed-exponential accuracy; quantile within `[min, max]`; merge element-wise add + min/max bounds + serialized-state round-trip + mismatched-`k` Ôćĺ error; config / value / `q` validation + `MomentSketchError.detail`; stats / reset / reconfigure; 8-thread concurrent adds; all 5 endpoints over HTTP incl. `DELETE`-with-body reset + a prior-phase regression check.
- Ôťů 106E: `scripts/prove.py` ÔÇö 229 test modules registered (Phase 106 appends `test_moment_sketch.py` + `test_moment_sketch_web.py`).
- Ôťů 106F: README Phase Map updated; Phase 107 planned.

**Phase 107 ÔÇö Complete.** All 231 test modules green. Sovereign Counting Bloom Filter ÔÇö a Bloom variant whose single-bit array is replaced by an array of small integer **counters**, which buys the one thing a classic Bloom cannot do: **deletion**. `add` increments each of an element's `k` hashed counters; `remove` decrements them (guarded by a membership check first, so an absent element raises rather than under-decrementing and corrupting genuine members' counts); `contains` reports membership when *every* hashed counter is `Ôëą 1`. Standard Bloom sizing ÔÇö `m = Ôîł-n┬Ěln(p)/(ln2)┬▓Ôîë` counters and `k = Ôîł(m/n)┬Ěln2Ôîë` hash functions for capacity `n` and target error_rate `p`. Counters are **4-bit-valued** (16 states `0..15`, one byte each in an `array.array('B')`) and `add` **saturates** at 15, so a hot element can never overflow and corrupt the structure (the bounded cost: exact deletion is lost only for an element added more than 15 times). Hashing is a **double-hashing** scheme `h_i(x) = (h1(x) + i┬Ěh2(x)) mod m` for `i = 0..k-1`, where `h1`/`h2` are the two halves of one seeded BLAKE2b digest (the same stable, process-independent folding idiom as MinHash P88). Like any Bloom it admits **false positives** (bounded by `error_rate`) but ÔÇö saturation aside ÔÇö **no false negatives**. Pure stdlib (`array` + `hashlib`); thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/counting_bloom_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- Ôťů 107A: `pradyos/core/counting_bloom.py` ÔÇö `CountingBloomError(detail)`; `CountingBloom(capacity=10000, error_rate=0.01, seed=0)` with `add(element)` (saturating increment), `contains(element)` / `__contains__`, `remove(element)` (decrement; raises `CountingBloomError("element not in filter")` if absent), `false_positive_rate()` (= `(1 - e^(-k┬Ěn/m))^k`), `reset(capacity=None, error_rate=None, seed=None)`, `__len__`, `capacity`/`error_rate`/`seed`/`num_hash_functions`/`num_counters`/`count` properties (`count` = number of `add` calls, *not* unique elements ÔÇö noted in the docstring), and `stats()` (capacity / error_rate / num_hash_functions / num_counters / count / false_positive_rate). Invalid `capacity` (Ôłë ÔäĄÔü║), `error_rate` (Ôłë (0,1)) or `seed` raise `CountingBloomError`.
- Ôťů 107B: `pradyos/web/counting_bloom_web.py` ÔÇö `register_countingbloom_routes(app, counting_bloom=None)` (defaults to a fresh per-app filter) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/countingbloom/add` (body `{element}`; 422 on missing element), `GET /api/v1/countingbloom/contains` (`?element=`), `POST /api/v1/countingbloom/remove` (body `{element}`; **400 when the element is absent** ÔÇö a state error, distinct from a 422 validation error), `GET /api/v1/countingbloom/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/countingbloom/reset` (body `{capacity?, error_rate?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).
- Ôťů 107C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase107.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `counting_bloom` param, and a single `register_countingbloom_routes(app, counting_bloom)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- Ôťů 107D: `tests/test_counting_bloom.py` (51) + `tests/test_countingbloom_web.py` (20) ÔÇö **FPR accuracy** (1 000 members, 10 000 non-member probes Ôćĺ measured FPR ÔëĄ 0.02); **no false negatives** (all 1 000 members contained); **deletion** (add Ôćĺ contains Ôćĺ remove Ôćĺ not contains); **double-add/single-remove** still present, **double-remove** gone; **no under-decrement corruption** (removing one element leaves 200 neighbours intact); **saturation** (add ├Ś20 Ôćĺ counter capped at 15, no crash, still contained); **remove-of-absent raises** `CountingBloomError`; standard Bloom sizing (`m`/`k` formulae; tighter error_rate grows `m`); FPR formula + grows-with-load + zero-when-empty; determinism (same seed Ôćĺ identical counter array; survives reset; insertion-order independent; different seed Ôćĺ different array); config validation + `CountingBloomError.detail`; stats / reset / reconfigure; 8-thread concurrent adds; all 5 endpoints over HTTP incl. `DELETE`-with-body reset + the absent-remove **400** + a prior-phase regression check.
- Ôťů 107E: `scripts/prove.py` ÔÇö 231 test modules registered (Phase 107 appends `test_counting_bloom.py` + `test_countingbloom_web.py`).

**Phase 108 ÔÇö Complete.** All 233 test modules green. Sovereign Binary Fuse Filter (Graf & Lemire, 2022 ÔÇö the segmented refinement of the fuse-graph construction, Dietzfelbinger & Walzer). Like the Phase 100 XOR filter it is a **static, space-optimal** approximate-membership filter built once from a complete key set; a query XORs three 8-bit fingerprint slots and compares against the key's own fingerprint, so there are **zero false negatives** and a false-positive rate of `Ôëł 2**-8 = 1/256 Ôëł 0.39 %`. Hashing is a single seeded **xxhash-style** 64-bit integer mix ÔÇö `mix(x, seed) = ((x ^ seed) ┬Ě 0x517cc1b727220a95) & MASK64` (pure Python, no external dependency) ÔÇö sliced into three segment-local indices `h_i = (mix >> 21┬Ěi) % segment` and a fingerprint `f = mix & 0xFF`; the three probed slots live in consecutive segments (`array[h0]`, `array[h1+seg]`, `array[h2+2┬Ěseg]`). Construction **peels** the 3-XOR hypergraph (repeatedly removing a slot touched by exactly one unassigned key) then assigns fingerprints in reverse peel order so each key's equation holds; peeling is probabilistic, so a stall triggers an **internal seed retry** (the seed is advanced deterministically, so a fixed key set still yields a reproducible filter). The filter is **immutable after build** ÔÇö there is no incremental `add`; `reset` returns it to the unbuilt state. Keys are sorted internally, so build order does not change the result. Pure stdlib (`hashlib` + integer mixing); thread-safe via a single `threading.RLock` (build and contains can race). Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/binary_fuse_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- Ôťů 108A: `pradyos/core/binary_fuse.py` ÔÇö `BinaryFuseError(detail)`; `BinaryFuseFilter(seed=0)` with `build(keys)` (static; sorts + dedups; `BinaryFuseError("duplicate keys")` on dups, `BinaryFuseError("build failed: cycle detected")` if peeling never converges across the internal seed retries), `contains(key)` / `__contains__` (`BinaryFuseError("filter not built")` before build), `reset(seed=None)` (back to unbuilt), `__len__`, `seed`/`built`/`array_size` properties, and `stats()` (built / num_keys / array_size / bits_per_key = `8┬Ěm/n` when built and non-empty else None / seed). Segments are sized at `Ôîł1.23┬Ěn/3Ôîë + 4` slots each (`m = 3┬Ěsegment`, Ôëł 9.9 bits/key) ÔÇö the regime where 3-segment peeling is reliable.
- Ôťů 108B: `pradyos/web/binary_fuse_web.py` ÔÇö `register_binaryfuse_routes(app, binary_fuse=None)` (defaults to a fresh unbuilt filter) mounts 4 (all-static) routes ÔÇö **no insert (the filter is static)**: `POST /api/v1/binaryfuse/build` (body `{keys: [...]}`; 422 on missing / non-list keys, **400** on duplicate / build cycle), `GET /api/v1/binaryfuse/contains` (`?key=`; **400 before build**), `GET /api/v1/binaryfuse/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/binaryfuse/reset` (body `{seed?}`; 422 on bad seed).
- Ôťů 108C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase108.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `binary_fuse` param, and a single `register_binaryfuse_routes(app, binary_fuse)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- Ôťů 108D: `tests/test_binary_fuse.py` (49) + `tests/test_binaryfuse_web.py` (20) ÔÇö **no false negatives** (every built key contained, small and large key sets); **FPR** ÔëĄ 0.005 over 10 000 non-member probes (Ôëł 1/256 theory); **space efficiency** (`bits_per_key ÔëĄ 10`, `array_size Ôëł 1.23┬Ěn + 12`); **determinism** (same seed + keys Ôćĺ identical array, survives retries) + **order-independence** (`build([a,b,c]) == build([c,a,b])`, incl. large reversed sets) + different-seed Ôćĺ different array; **immutability** (no `add`; rebuild replaces); duplicate-keys / not-built / cycle Ôćĺ `BinaryFuseError`; build across sizes `n = 1..3000`; reset Ôćĺ unbuilt + contains raises + rebuildable; 8-thread concurrent `contains`; all 4 endpoints over HTTP incl. `DELETE`-with-body reset, the build-duplicate **400**, the contains-before-build **400**, + a prior-phase regression check.
- Ôťů 108E: `scripts/prove.py` ÔÇö 233 test modules registered (Phase 108 appends `test_binary_fuse.py` + `test_binaryfuse_web.py`).

**Phase 109 ÔÇö Complete.** All 235 test modules green. Sovereign Vacuum Filter (Wang, Zhou, Yang, Du, Yang & Uhlig, 2019) ÔÇö a space-efficient approximate-membership filter in the **cuckoo-fingerprint** family (cf. the Phase 86 cuckoo filter) supporting both **insertion** and **deletion** while using *less* space than the cuckoo filter at the same false-positive rate. The cuckoo filter recovers an item's alternate bucket by `i2 = i1 XOR H(fp)`, which is an involution over `[0, m)` **only when the bucket count `m` is rounded up to a power of two** ÔÇö wasting on average ~1.5├Ś (up to 2├Ś) the space actually needed. The Vacuum Filter removes that constraint with an **Alternate Range** `L` (a power of two): both candidate buckets are confined to the same `L`-aligned *chunk* of `L` consecutive buckets via `i2 = i1 XOR (H(fp) mod L)`. Because `H(fp) mod L < L` flips only the low `log2(L)` bits, `i1` and `i2` always share the chunk `[ÔîŐi1/LÔîő┬ĚL, ÔîŐi1/LÔîő┬ĚL + L)`; the bucket count then only has to be a **multiple of `L`** (`m = num_chunks ┬Ě L`) rather than a power of two, so it sits much closer to the true required size (measured **18ÔÇô44 % smaller** than the cuckoo filter's next-power-of-two across n = 1.1kÔÇô100k). Each chunk is an independent power-of-two cuckoo sub-table, so intra-chunk partial-key kicking reaches high occupancy (**Ôëł 0.95 load** at first insert failure, measured) while the chunk count absorbs the rest at fine granularity. The XOR stays an involution because `ÔîŐi1/LÔîő┬ĚL` is a multiple of `L` (low bits zero) and `m` is a multiple of `L` (so `chunk_base + L ÔëĄ m`), and the displacement depends only on the fingerprint ÔÇö so a kicked fingerprint **never leaves its origin chunk** and the filter **never reports a false negative** (a failed insert is rolled back atomically), while `contains` may false-positive at `Ôëł 2┬Ěbucket_size / 2^fingerprint_bits` exactly as the cuckoo filter does. The hash is injectable (`hash_fn`) for deterministic tests, with a `seed` salting the default stable BLAKE2b fold (process-independent). Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock` (the public surface acquires it; internal helpers under the lock never re-acquire it). Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/vacuum_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- Ôťů 109A: `pradyos/core/vacuum_filter.py` ÔÇö `VacuumFilterError(detail)`; `VacuumFilter(capacity, bucket_size=4, fingerprint_bits=8, max_kicks=500, alt_range=None, seed=0, hash_fn=None)` with `insert(item)` (partial-key cuckoo kicking confined to the item's chunk; atomic rollback Ôćĺ returns `False` when the chunk is full), `contains(item)` / `__contains__`, `delete(item)` (removes one fingerprint; `False` if absent), `reset()`, `__len__`, and `capacity` (bucket count = `num_chunks┬Ěalt_range`) / `alt_range` / `num_chunks` / `seed` properties, plus `stats()` (capacity / num_chunks / alt_range / count / load_factor / fingerprint_bits / max_kicks). `alt_range` defaults to an auto-chosen power of two (~8 large chunks) and is validated as a power of two (and clamped to fit `capacity`); invalid `capacity` / `bucket_size` / `fingerprint_bits` (>32) / `max_kicks` / `seed` / `alt_range` raise `VacuumFilterError` (bools rejected).
- Ôťů 109B: `pradyos/web/vacuum_web.py` ÔÇö `register_vacuum_routes(app, vacuum_filter=None)` (defaults to a fresh `VacuumFilter` cap 1024) mounts 5 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/vacuum/insert` (body `{item}`; 422 on missing / non-dict body), `POST /api/v1/vacuum/contains` (body `{item}`; 422 on missing), `DELETE /api/v1/vacuum/delete` (body `{item}`; 422 on missing), `GET /api/v1/vacuum/stats`, `POST /api/v1/vacuum/reset`.
- Ôťů 109C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase109.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `vacuum_filter` param, and a single `register_vacuum_routes(app, vacuum_filter)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- Ôťů 109D: `tests/test_vacuum_filter.py` (61) + `tests/test_vacuum_web.py` (20) ÔÇö **no false negatives** (every inserted key contained, small sets and high-occupancy fills); **involution + chunk confinement** (`alt(alt(i,fp),fp)==i`, `i1`/`i2` share the `L`-aligned chunk, both in `[0,m)` over thousands of keys); **space efficiency** (`m` a multiple of `alt_range`, `m == num_chunks┬Ěalt_range`, `m ÔëĄ next_pow2(capacity)` at every size and strictly `<` for non-power-of-two chunk counts ÔÇö `cap=3000 Ôćĺ m=3072 < 4096`); **high occupancy** (Ôëą 0.90 load before first failure, zero false negatives); **FPR** (default hash, 8-bit fp, `b=4` Ôćĺ measured ÔëĄ 0.05 over the ~3.1 % theory) + **wider fingerprint** (16-bit Ôćĺ ÔëĄ 0.005); **deletion** (insert Ôćĺ contains Ôćĺ delete Ôćĺ absent; reinsert; injected-collision false-positive clears on delete); **determinism** (injected hash and same-`seed` reproducible; different `seed` diverges placement); auto/explicit `alt_range` layout (`cap=3000 Ôćĺ L=256, 12 chunks`; `cap=4096 Ôćĺ L=512, 8 chunks`); full-chunk rollback (no corruption, count unchanged); config validation + `VacuumFilterError.detail`; stats / reset / reset-preserves-layout; 10-thread concurrent inserts + concurrent insert/delete; all 5 endpoints over HTTP incl. `DELETE`-with-body delete + deterministic FP-and-clear + a prior-phase regression check (now incl. `binaryfuse`).
- Ôťů 109E: `scripts/prove.py` ÔÇö 235 test modules registered (Phase 109 appends `test_vacuum_filter.py` + `test_vacuum_web.py`).
- Ôťů 109F: README Phase Map updated; Phase 110 planned.

**Phase 110 ÔÇö Complete.** All 237 test modules green. Sovereign Stable Bloom Filter (Deng & Rafiei, SIGMOD 2006) ÔÇö a Bloom variant for **unbounded data streams**. A classic Bloom (Phase 72) or Counting Bloom (Phase 107) **saturates** on an endless stream: every cell eventually fills, the false-positive rate climbs to 1, and the filter is useless. The Stable Bloom Filter fixes this by **continuously forgetting** ÔÇö it stores an array of small `d`-bit **cells** (each in `0..Max`, `Max = 2^d Ôłĺ 1`) and on *every* insertion first **decrements `P` uniformly-random cells** (floored at 0) before **setting the element's `k` hashed cells to `Max`**. The decrement step evicts stale information at a constant rate, so the count of zero cells converges to a non-zero steady state regardless of stream length ÔÇö the fill ratio (and hence the FP rate) **stabilises** instead of growing (measured: fill plateaus at **~0.58** across 5kÔćĺ120k inserts, never saturating). `contains` reports membership when every one of an element's `k` cells is `Ôëą 1`; because a set cell can later be decremented to 0, the filter admits a small **bounded false-negative** rate for *old* elements (recent inserts recalled with ~1.0 probability; stale items measured ~0.87 forgotten after flooding) ÔÇö the deliberate price for bounded memory on an infinite stream, and exactly what separates it from the no-false-negative Bloom family. `P` defaults to `num_hashes ┬Ě max_value` (the balance point where mass removed Ôëł mass added), tunable for a tighter FP/FN trade (Deng & Rafiei derive the optimal `P` from a target stable FP). Cells are one byte each in an `array.array('B')` (`Max ÔëĄ 255`); hashing is double-hashing `h_i = (h1 + i┬Ěh2) mod m` from one seeded BLAKE2b digest (the MinHash/Counting-Bloom idiom); the eviction draws from a `random.Random(seed)` so a fixed seed + insertion sequence reproduce the filter exactly. Pure stdlib (`array` + `hashlib` + `random`); thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/stable_bloom_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- Ôťů 110A: `pradyos/core/stable_bloom.py` ÔÇö `StableBloomError(detail)`; `StableBloomFilter(num_cells=10000, num_hashes=5, max_value=3, decrement=None, seed=0)` with `add(element)` (evict `P` random cells then set `k` cells to `Max`), `contains(element)` / `__contains__`, `fill_ratio()` (fraction of non-zero cells), `reset(...)` (clear / reconfigure; re-seeds the eviction RNG), `__len__`, and `num_cells` / `num_hashes` / `max_value` / `decrement` (P) / `seed` / `count` properties, plus `stats()` (num_cells / num_hashes / max_value / decrement / count / fill_ratio / seed). `decrement` defaults to `min(num_hashes┬Ěmax_value, num_cells)`; invalid `num_cells` / `num_hashes` / `max_value` (Ôłë 1..255) / `decrement` (Ôłë 1..num_cells) / `seed` raise `StableBloomError` (bools rejected).
- Ôťů 110B: `pradyos/web/stable_bloom_web.py` ÔÇö `register_stablebloom_routes(app, stable_bloom=None)` (defaults to a fresh `StableBloomFilter`) mounts 4 (all-static) routes ÔÇö **no remove (the filter forgets on its own)**: `POST /api/v1/stablebloom/add` (body `{element}`; 422 on missing / non-dict), `GET /api/v1/stablebloom/contains` (`?element=`), `GET /api/v1/stablebloom/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/stablebloom/reset` (body `{num_cells?, num_hashes?, max_value?, decrement?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).
- Ôťů 110C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase110.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `stable_bloom` param, and a single `register_stablebloom_routes(app, stable_bloom)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- Ôťů 110D: `tests/test_stable_bloom.py` (43) + `tests/test_stablebloom_web.py` (18) ÔÇö **fresh add recalled**; **empty contains Ôćĺ False**; **stability** (fill plateaus over a 40k stream, never `Ôëą 0.95`); **recent recall** (`Ôëą 0.95`); **forgetting** (stale victims evicted after flooding, FN_old `Ôëą 0.5`); **FP bounded** (`< 0.20` after warmup); **no saturation** under heavy stream; **larger `max_value` Ôçĺ higher recall**; **determinism** (same seed + sequence Ôćĺ identical stats & membership; different seed diverges; reset re-seeds the RNG); default/explicit `decrement` (k┬ĚMax, capped at num_cells); config validation + `StableBloomError.detail` (incl. `max_value > 255`, `decrement > num_cells`, bools); stats / properties / fill_ratio; reset clears + reconfigures; 10-thread concurrent adds + concurrent add/contains; all 4 endpoints over HTTP incl. `DELETE`-with-body reset + a prior-phase regression check (now incl. `vacuum`).
- Ôťů 110E: `scripts/prove.py` ÔÇö 237 test modules registered (Phase 110 appends `test_stable_bloom.py` + `test_stablebloom_web.py`).
- Ôťů 110F: README Phase Map updated; Phase 111 planned.

**Phase 111 ÔÇö Complete.** All 239 test modules green. Sovereign Morris Counter (Morris, 1978 ÔÇö *Counting large numbers of events in small registers*) ÔÇö the original **approximate counting** algorithm. Counting to `n` exactly needs `ÔîłlogÔéé nÔîë` bits; the Morris counter stores only a small **exponent register** `c` and reaches an estimate of `n` in `Ôëł logÔéé logÔéé n` bits by incrementing `c` only *probabilistically*. For the generalised base `a > 1` (Flajolet 1985): on each event `c ÔćÉ c + 1` with probability `a^(Ôłĺc)`, and the estimate is `n╠é = (a^c Ôłĺ 1)/(a Ôłĺ 1)`. The estimate is **unbiased** ÔÇö `E[n╠é] = n` for all `n` ÔÇö which follows by induction (`E[a^c]` rises by exactly `a Ôłĺ 1` per event, so `E[a^c] = 1 + n┬Ě(a Ôłĺ 1)`); the classic **base-2** case is the familiar `increment with prob 2^(Ôłĺc)`, `n╠é = 2^c Ôłĺ 1`. The base trades memory for accuracy (variance `Ôëł n┬Ě(n Ôłĺ 1)┬Ě(a Ôłĺ 1)/2`): a base near 1 is very accurate but the register grows almost like an exact counter, while a larger base keeps the register tiny at higher variance (measured: base-2 register `c = 16` for `n = 100 000`; mean estimate over 400 seeds within ~5 % of `n`; mean |rel error| 0.17 at base 1.1 vs 0.47 at base 2.0). This is a **new feature-class** ÔÇö *approximate counting* ÔÇö distinct from the cardinality sketches (HyperLogLog/P74, Theta/P93, which count *distinct* items) and the frequency sketches (Count-Min/P76, Count-Sketch/P94, per-key counts): the Morris counter estimates a single running **event total**. The compact state is the single integer `register`; an exact `increments` tally is kept only so `stats`/`relative_error` can report observed accuracy (a memory-constrained deployment would omit it). The probabilistic coin is a `random.Random(seed)`, so a fixed seed + increment sequence reproduce the counter exactly. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/morris_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- Ôťů 111A: `pradyos/core/morris_counter.py` ÔÇö `MorrisCounterError(detail)`; `MorrisCounter(base=2.0, seed=0)` with `increment(times=1)` (each event bumps `c` with prob `base^(Ôłĺc)`; returns the new register; `MorrisCounterError` on `times Ôłë ÔäĄÔü║`), `estimate()` (`(base^c Ôłĺ 1)/(base Ôłĺ 1)`), `relative_error()` (`|estimate Ôłĺ increments|/increments`, 0 when empty), `reset(base=None, seed=None)` (re-seeds the RNG), and `register` (c) / `increments` (exact n) / `base` / `seed` properties, plus `stats()` (register / estimate / increments / base / relative_error / seed). Invalid `base` (Ôłë (1, Ôł×)) or `seed` raise `MorrisCounterError` (bools rejected; `int` base coerced to `float`).
- Ôťů 111B: `pradyos/web/morris_web.py` ÔÇö `register_morris_routes(app, morris_counter=None)` (defaults to a fresh `MorrisCounter`) mounts 4 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/morris/increment` (body `{times?}`, default 1; **422** on `times Ôłë ÔäĄÔü║`), `GET /api/v1/morris/estimate` (`{estimate, register}`), `GET /api/v1/morris/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/morris/reset` (body `{base?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).
- Ôťů 111C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase111.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `morris_counter` param, and a single `register_morris_routes(app, morris_counter)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- Ôťů 111D: `tests/test_morris_counter.py` (41) + `tests/test_morris_web.py` (19) ÔÇö **unbiasedness** (mean estimate over 400 seeds within 10 % of `n` at base 2, within 8 % at base 1.5); **log-log register** (`c < 30` for `n = 100 000`); **base-2 formula** (`estimate == 2^c Ôłĺ 1`) + **general-base formula**; **smaller base lowers variance** (mean |rel error| base 1.1 < base 2.0); **determinism** (same seed + sequence Ôćĺ identical register/estimate; `increment(n)` Ôëí `n├Śincrement(1)`; different seed diverges; reset re-seeds); **monotonic** register; validation (`base ÔëĄ 1`, non-number, bools, `times Ôłł {0, Ôłĺ5, 2.5, "x"}`) + `MorrisCounterError.detail`; properties; relative_error (mean Ôëł 0.25 at base 1.2) / stats / reset; 10-thread concurrent increments (exact tally under the lock); all 4 endpoints over HTTP incl. `DELETE`-with-body reset + a prior-phase regression check (now incl. `stablebloom`).

**Phase 112 ÔÇö Complete.** All 241 test modules green. Sovereign Linear Counting (Whang, Vander-Zanden & Taylor, 1990 ÔÇö *A linear-time probabilistic counting algorithm for database applications*) ÔÇö a **cardinality** (distinct-count) estimator markedly more accurate than HyperLogLog at *small-to-moderate* cardinalities, for more space. The structure is one **bitmap** of `m` bits; each item is hashed to one position `h(x) mod m` and that bit is set, so duplicates collapse and the bitmap depends only on the *distinct* items. After the stream, the count is estimated from the **fraction of still-zero bits** `V = zero_bits/m`: `n╠é = Ôłĺm┬Ěln(V)`. The derivation is the balls-in-bins empty-bin expectation ÔÇö a bit is zero iff no distinct item hashed to it, so `E[zero_bits] = m┬Ě(1 Ôłĺ 1/m)^n Ôëł m┬Ěe^(Ôłĺn/m)`, giving `E[V] Ôëł e^(Ôłĺn/m)` and `n Ôëł Ôłĺm┬Ěln(V)` (measured: sub-1 % relative error to load ~0.8; zero-bit count within 0.1 % of `m┬Ěe^(Ôłĺn/m)`). Once **every** bit is set the bitmap is *saturated*, `V = 0`, and the estimate is undefined ÔÇö `estimate()` raises `LinearCounterError`. This is a *different* cardinality algorithm from HyperLogLog (P74 ÔÇö maximum leading-zero registers) and the Theta sketch (P93 ÔÇö KMV / k-minimum-values): bitmap-and-empty-bins rather than order statistics, matching the one-algorithm-per-method pattern. Hashing is a single seeded BLAKE2b digest; a running set-bit count keeps `estimate` O(1). Pure stdlib (`hashlib`); thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/linear_counter_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- Ôťů 112A: `pradyos/core/linear_counter.py` ÔÇö `LinearCounterError(detail)`; `LinearCounter(num_bits=65536, seed=0)` with `add(item)` (idempotent bit-set; distinct-count semantics), `add_many(items)` (`LinearCounterError` on a non-iterable), `estimate()` (`Ôłĺm┬Ěln(V)`; **raises when saturated**), `reset(num_bits=None, seed=None)`, `load_factor()`, `__len__` (bits set), and `num_bits` (m) / `bits_set` / `seed` / `saturated` properties, plus `stats()` (num_bits / bits_set / zero_bits / load_factor / estimate (None if saturated) / seed). Invalid `num_bits` (Ôłë ÔäĄÔü║) or `seed` raise `LinearCounterError` (bools rejected).
- Ôťů 112B: `pradyos/web/linear_counter_web.py` ÔÇö `register_linearcounting_routes(app, linear_counter=None)` (defaults to a fresh `LinearCounter`) mounts 4 (all-static) routes: `POST /api/v1/linearcounting/add` (body `{element}`; 422 on missing / non-dict), `GET /api/v1/linearcounting/estimate` (`{estimate, bits_set}`; **400 when saturated** ÔÇö a state error), `GET /api/v1/linearcounting/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/linearcounting/reset` (body `{num_bits?, seed?}`; 422 on bad config).
- Ôťů 112C: `pradyos/sovereign_web.py` patched additively via `scripts/patch_web_phase112.py` (+4 lines: the import, the `linear_counter` param, and a single `register_linearcounting_routes(app, linear_counter)` call before `return app`; the DASHBOARD_HTML line is asserted byte-length-unchanged; an `ast.parse` gate refuses to write broken code). Existing routes untouched.
- Ôťů 112D: `tests/test_linear_counter.py` (35) + `tests/test_linearcounting_web.py` (17) ÔÇö **accuracy** (rel error `< 0.03` at loads 0.07 / 0.26 / 0.53 / 0.76); **idempotent distinct-count** (1000├Ś the same item Ôćĺ estimate Ôëł 1; 3000 distinct from 15 000 adds Ôćĺ Ôëł 3000); **zero-bit law** (measured zeros within 2 % of `m┬Ěe^(Ôłĺn/m)`); **larger `m` lowers error**; **saturation** (`saturated` flag + `estimate()` raises + `stats.estimate is None`); **determinism** (same seed Ôćĺ identical bitmap/estimate; different seed diverges the bitmap but the estimate stays within 5 %); config validation + `add_many` non-iterable + `LinearCounterError.detail`; properties / load_factor / stats; reset clears + reconfigures + re-add; 10-thread concurrent adds (estimate within 5 % of 5000 distinct); all 4 endpoints over HTTP incl. the saturated **400**, `DELETE`-with-body reset + a prior-phase regression check (now incl. `morris`).

**Phase 113 ÔÇö Complete.** All 243 test modules green. Sovereign Treap (Seidel & Aragon, 1996 ÔÇö *Randomized search trees*) ÔÇö a **randomized balanced binary search tree**. Each node is simultaneously BST-ordered by `key` and max-heap-ordered by a **random priority**; the heap constraint forces a unique tree shape ÔÇö the one a plain BST would take if keys were inserted in decreasing-priority order ÔÇö and since the priorities are random, that order is a uniformly random permutation, so the tree behaves like a BST built from random insertions: **expected height `Ôëł 2┬Ěln n`** and `search` / `insert` / `delete` / `rank` / `select` all `O(log n)` *expected*, with no balance-factor or colour bookkeeping. `insert` does a BST insert then rotates the new node up while its priority exceeds its parent's; `delete` removes a node by **merging its two subtrees** (higher-priority child becomes the local root, recursively). Every node stores its **subtree size**, making the order-statistics `rank(key)` (keys strictly smaller) and `select(i)` (the `i`-th smallest key) run in `O(log n)`. Measured: height 32 for `n = 5000` random keys (`2┬Ěln n Ôëł 17`), and ÔÇö the key property ÔÇö **sorted inserts stay balanced** (height 28, where a plain BST would be 5000) because random priorities defeat adversarial order. This is a *different* probabilistic ordered structure from the Skip List (P78, randomized tower levels over a linked list) ÔÇö random priorities + rotations over a tree ÔÇö matching the one-algorithm-per-method pattern. Priorities come from a seeded `random.Random` so a fixed seed + insertion sequence reproduce the tree exactly. Pure stdlib; thread-safe via a single `threading.Lock`. Routes live in their own `pradyos/web/treap_web.py` module, wired into `create_app()` factory scope:

- Ôťů 113A: `pradyos/core/treap.py` ÔÇö `TreapError(detail)`; `Treap(seed=0)` with `insert(key, value=None)` (BST insert + rotate-up; updates value in place on a duplicate, no growth), `delete(key)` Ôćĺ bool (subtree merge), `contains(key)` / `__contains__`, `search(key)` (raises if absent) / `get(key, default=None)`, `rank(key)`, `select(index)` (raises out of range), `min_key()` / `max_key()` (raise when empty), `keys()` (in-order, iterative), `height()`, `reset(seed=None)` (re-seeds priorities), `__len__`, and `seed` property, plus `stats()` (size / height / min / max / seed). Invalid `seed` raises `TreapError` (bools rejected); every node keeps a maintained `size`.
- Ôťů 113B: `pradyos/web/treap_web.py` ÔÇö `register_treap_routes(app, treap=None)` (defaults to a fresh `Treap`) mounts 7 (all-static) routes with **numeric keys** (so the order statistics have a total order): `POST /api/v1/treap/insert` (body `{key, value?}`; 422 on missing / non-numeric key), `DELETE /api/v1/treap/delete` (body `{key}`; 422 on bad key), `GET /api/v1/treap/search` (`?key=`), `GET /api/v1/treap/rank` (`?key=`), `GET /api/v1/treap/select` (`?index=` `Query(ge=0)`; **400 when out of range** ÔÇö a state error), `GET /api/v1/treap/stats`, `DELETE /api/v1/treap/reset` (body `{seed?}`).

Existing routes untouched.
